1. Introduction
  



   1. Purpose of this document
This document provides the specification for B2B XML request and response between client’s server and Credit Bureau Malaysia System Server.




   2. Audience
This document is intended for:
* Users’ representatives and project team members of Credit Bureau Malaysia.


   3. Terms and Standards
The following tabulates the terms and standards used across this document


Terms and Standard
	Definition
	SSM
	Suruhanjaya Syarikat-syarikat Malaysia
	CCRIS
	Central Credit Reference Information System
	DCHEQS
	Dishonoured Cheque Information System
	CBM
	Credit Bureau Malaysia
	CBMS
	Credit Bureau Malaysia System
	Subject
	SME Entity that is enquired upon
	BIP or Interest Party(ies)
	Owner/Partner/Director/Shareholder/Guarantor

2. System Overview
  





   5. B2B Process Flow
      1. Report Enquiry (BIR, BIR-P, CLR)
The report enquiry flow (BIR, BIR-P, CLR) for SCBS is shown as diagram below:          




  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  





Full cycle of report enquiry (BIR, BIR-P, CLR) consists of 2 XML requests and 2 XML responses as below:


         1. XML Request from member to start the report enquiry (refer 3.1.1)
         2. XML Response to return the Subject Listing (refer 3.1.2)
         3. XML Request from member to confirm the Subject (refer 3.1.3)
         4. XML Response with the Report Details. XML response will be based on purchased report type. (refer 3.1.4)
         5. XML Request from member to retry Report Details retrieval if there was a connection or timeout failure for step viii (refer 3.1.5)
         6. XML Response with the Report Details (if found). XML response will be based on request number for previous request. (refer 3.1.6)


The full cycle above is considering as 1 case.
      2. Report Enquiry (Other)


The report enquiry flow (other) for SCBS is shown as diagram below:                                  


























































Full cycle of report enquiry (other) consists of 3 XML requests and 3 XML responses as below:      


7. XML Request from member to start the report enquiry (refer 3.2.1)
8. XML Response to return the Subject Listing (refer 3.2.2)
9. XML Request from member to confirm the Subject (refer 3.2.3)
10. XML Response to return the Business Interest Party(ies) (refer 3.2.4)
11. XML Request from member to add Business Interest Party(ies) (refer 3.2.3)
12. XML Response to return the newly added Business Interest Party(ies) (refer 3.2.4)
13. XML Request from member to confirm the Business Interest Party(ies) (refer 3.2.5)
14. XML Response with the Report Details. XML response will be based on purchased report type (refer 3.2.6)
15. XML Request from member to retry Report Details retrieval if there was a connection or timeout failure for step viii (refer 3.2.7)
16. XML Response with the Report Details (if found). XML response will be based on request number for previous request. (refer 3.2.8)


The full cycle above is considering as 1 case.


   6. Products and Services
The available products and services are:


1. Business Information Report (BIR)
2. Business Information Report Premium (BIR-P)
3. Business Review Report (BRR)
4. Business Review Report Premium (BRR-P)
5. Credit Risk Report (CRR)
6. Credit Risk Report Premium (CRR-P)
7. Credit Risk Report Lite (CRR-LITE)
8. Corporate Link Report (CLR)
9. Business Assessment Report – Company (BAR-C)
10. Business Assessment Report – Business (BAR-B)
11. Credit Risk Report Supplementary (CRR-SUP)
12. Credit Risk Report Supplementary Premium (CRR-SUP-P)
13. Credit Risk Report X Lite A (CRR-XLITE-A)
14. Credit Risk Report Property Premium (CRR-PROP-P)
15. Credit Risk Report Property Plus Premium (CRR-PROP-PLUS-P)
16. Credit Risk Report II (CRR-II)
17. Credit Risk Report Premium II (CRR-P-II)


* Please refer to www.creditbureau.com.my for more details and sample reports.






   7. Member’s Preparation for B2B Interface
In order for member to have an automatic data exchange procedures (request and response) to/from SCBS platform via the B2B interface, the member needs to have the following standard and automated processes to:


1. Members are required to register a B2B user with SCBS.
2. Only authorized member’s IP is allowed to interface to SCBS.
3. Member needs to provide the IP before B2B to interface. SCBS will only allow authorized IP to access SCBS B2B Interface.
4. Members are required to install the trusted certificate on B2B server issued by SCBS.
5. Online Request data will post via HTTPS to SCBS.
6. URL of B2B services will be issued by SCBS to member upon approval of B2B user.

<SequenceNo>001</SequenceNo>

</Subject>

<Request>

<Service>SMEDTLRPTS</Service>
<ReportType>BIR</ReportType>
<MemberID>AA0001</MemberID>
<UserID>AA00010001</UserID>
<ReqNo>20080311000001</ReqNo>
<!-- Request Number, format: yyyymmddnnnnnn, nnnnnn is a running number -->
<SequenceNo>002</SequenceNo>
<ReqDate></ReqDate>
<PurposeStdCode></PurposeStdCode>
<CostCenterStdCode></CostCenterStdCode>
<ConsentFlag></ConsentFlag>
<Subject>
<RegNo></RegNo>
<RegName></RegName>
<DateBR></DateBR>
<ConstitutionTypeStdCode></ConstitutionTypeStdCode>
<EmailAddr>XXXXXXXX</EmailAddr>
<MobileNo>XXXXXXXXXXX</MobileNo>
<BusinessCouCodeStdCode></BusinessCouCodeStdCode>
<BusinessStaCodeStdCode></BusinessStaCodeStdCode>
<EntityCode>1</EntityCode>
<TradeEntityCode></TradeEntityCode>
<Warning></Warning>
</Subject>
<InterestParties/>
</Request>

	Data Type

4. Error Details
  





The error details for SME Credit Bureau B2B services are:


Error Details
	Verification Process
	001 - Invalid Request XML
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	002 - Invalid IP Address
	Check with network administrator on the network setting. Make sure the IP address is same as per registered with SME Credit
Bureau.
	003 - Invalid member / account expired
	Contact Credit Bureau Operation to renew the account
	004 - Invalid User / Password
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	005 - Member didn’t subscribed to requested product / Invalid Services
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	006 - Missing Mandatory Field
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	007 - Invalid Field Format
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	008 - Invalid Standard Code
	Verify Standard Code on Request XML and resend.
	009 – Duplicate Request Number
	Verify Request Number on Request XML and resend.
	010 - B2B Services Unavailable
	Contact Credit Bureau Operation or retry in 30 minutes
	011 -Response not found in Inbox
	Verify Request Number or retry in another 15 minutes.
	012 -Invalid Report Type / Request Number
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	013 -Invalid Member / Request Number
	Verify Request XML and resend.
	014 – No One-To-One Match Found For The Given Business Registration Number
	Verify Entity in the Request XML and resend.
	015 – No Record
	Verify entity and resend or Contact Credit Bureau Operation
	016 – Invalid Constitution Type
	Verify Constitution Type and resend.
	017 – D’Cheques System is not available
	Use sequence number 005 to retrieve supplementary report
	018 – Consent is required
	Consent is required for CCRIS related reports
	019 – Use sequence number 004 to retrieve the huge report
	Use sequence number 004 to retrieve the huge report in 30 minutes
	020 – Business Interest Party is not allowed
	Business Interest Party is not allowed
	021 – Staging SSM data is outdated (more than 2 years), Kindly please proceed to purchase Premium Report
	Report is not allowed to be generated with staging SSM data is more than 2 years.
Please proceed to purchase premium report.
	025 - You are not allowed to retrieve report for this SME. Please contact Bureau for more details.
	You are not allowed to retrieve report for this
SME. Please contact Bureau for more details.
	026 - You are not allowed to retrieve report for this SME. Please contact Security Admin for more details.
	You are not allowed to retrieve report for this SME. Please contact Security Admin for more details.
	027 – No record in SSM for this subject. Please try purchasing CRR.
	No record in SSM for this subject. Please try purchasing CRR.
	



099 - Data Source Services Unavailable
	Contact Credit Bureau Operation or retry in 30 minutes
	999 - Others
	Contact Credit Bureau Operation or retry in 30 minutes
	

5. Warning Details
  



The warning details for SME Credit Bureau B2B services are:


Warning Details
	Verification Process
	At the time this report was extracted, DCHEQS was not available. Kindly retry request with Sequence 005, during DCHEQS available hours
from 9AM to 10PM, Monday to Friday.
	Use sequence number 005 to retrieve supplementary report
	

6. Sample Code
  





Member can use the following sample code to retrieve the XML response from SCBS:


// Request XML String request =  
"<Request><SystemID>SCBS</SystemID><ReqNo>20080311000001</ReqNo><SequenceNo>00 1</SequenceNo><ReqDate>12052008 141210</ReqDate><Services><CCRIS>SMEENTLSTS</CCRIS><DCheqs>SMEENTLSTS</DCheqs>
<SSMStaging>SMEENTLSTS</SSMStaging><EInfo>N</EInfo><Trade>SMEENTLSTS</Trade><S MERating>N</SMERating></Services><Subject><RegNo/><RegName/><DateBR/><Constitu tionType/><BusinessCouCode/><BusinessStaCode/><EntityCode/></Subject></Request
>";


//Connect to B2B Services
// URL will be issued via email to member
URL urlObj = new URL("http://url/scbs/B2BServiceAction.do "); HttpURLConnection urlConn = (HttpURLConnection)urlObj.openConnection(); urlConn.setDoInput(true);
urlConn.setDoOutput(true);
urlConn.setRequestProperty(“Content-Type”, “text/xml”);


BufferedWriter writer = new BufferedWriter(new OutputStreamWriter(urlConn.getOutputStream()));
writer.write(request); writer.flush();


// Read XML Response
BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(urlConn.getInputStream()));
StringBuilder response = new StringBuilder(); String inputLine = null;
while( (inputLine = reader.readLine()) != null ) response.append(inputLine);


writer.close(); reader.close();


// Output of XML Response System.out.println(response);
